PART I : SEC. (I) - GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA - 02.03.2010
1 A
(Published by  Authority)
PART I : SECTION (I)  — GENERAL
Government Notifications
THE   PARLIAMENTARY  ELECTIONS  ACT,  No.  1  OF  1981
Notice Under Section 24(1)
GENERAL  ELECTIONS  OF  MEMBERS  OF  THE  PARLIAMENT
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 24(1) of the Parliamentary Elections Act, No. 1 of 1981 that —
(a) the election of Members of the Parliament in each of the Electoral Districts specified in the Schedule hereto, is
contested;
(b) the order in which the name of each recognized Political Party and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group and the symbol allotted to each such Party or Group appear in the ballot paper of each such Electoral District
shall be the same order as given in the Schedule hereto;
(c) the names of candidates (as indicated by the candidates) of each recognized Political Party or Independent Group,
placed in alphabetical order in accordance with the Sinhala alphabet, nominated for election as Members of Parliament
from each such Electoral District and the serial number assigned to each candidate, are as specified in the Schedule
hereto;
(d) the poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 08.04.2010 in each such Electoral District; and
(e) the situation of the polling station or stations for each of the polling districts in each such Electoral District, and the
particular polling stations, if any reserved for female voters, are as specified in the Schedule hereto.
DAYANANDA DISSANAYAKE,
Comissioner of Elections.
Election Secretariat,
Sarana Mawatha,
Rajagiriya.
02nd March, 2010.
N.B. - Sinhala and Tamil versions of this Gazette Extraordinary will be published separately.
EXTRAORDINARY
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
